I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `6.531365700567425*epsilon**3 - 0.6867651335523405*(T - 289.08080514174986) + 3.018423785145038*(T - 289.08080514174986)*log(epsilon + 1)`

Let me expand this:
- `6.531*epsilon**3 - 0.6868*T + 198.55 + 3.018*T*log(epsilon+1) - 872.56*log(epsilon+1)`

So GT = `6.531*epsilon**3 + 3.018*T*log(epsilon+1) - 0.6868*T - 872.56*log(epsilon+1) + 198.55`

The key basis functions are:
1. `epsilon**3`
2. `T*log(epsilon+1)`
3. `T` (linear in T, constant in epsilon)
4. `log(epsilon+1)`
5. Constant

Let me check each candidate systematically. For epsilon ≥ 0, `Abs(epsilon) = epsilon`.

**Key structural requirements:** The GT has `epsilon**3` which is very specific. Many candidates use `exp(c*epsilon)` which cannot exactly reproduce `epsilon**3` unless combined with other terms in a way that cancels to leave a polynomial. Let me focus on candidates that have `epsilon**3` explicitly or can generate it.

Let me scan for candidates with `epsilon**3` or `epsilon**c` terms:

- **Candidate 4:** Has `c8*epsilon**3` ✓, plus `T*c0*epsilon`, `T*c1*sin(...)`, `c4*epsilon**2`, `c5`, `c6*exp(c7*epsilon)`. The `T*c1*sin(c2*epsilon+c3)` cannot produce `T*log(epsilon+1)`. **NO MATCH**

- **Candidate 17:** `T*c0*epsilon + c1*epsilon**2 + c2 + c3*exp(c4*epsilon) + c5*log(c6*Abs(epsilon)+1) + c7*epsilon**c8*log(c9*Abs(epsilon)+1)`. Set c8=3, c9→∞ won't work. Actually `c7*epsilon**c8*log(c9*epsilon+1)`: if c8=0, this gives `c7*log(c9*epsilon+1)`. We need `T*log(epsilon+1)` but there's no T multiplying this term. **NO MATCH**

- **Candidate 30:** Has `T*c1*epsilon**3`. This gives T*epsilon**3, but GT has just epsilon**3 (no T). **NO MATCH** unless c1=0, but then we lose epsilon**3.

- **Candidate 43:** Has `T*c4*epsilon**2` but no epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

Let me look for candidates that have both `T*log(epsilon+1)` and `epsilon**3`:

- **Candidate 35:** `T*c0*epsilon + c1*epsilon**2 + c2*exp(c3*epsilon) + c4*log(c5*Abs(epsilon)+1) + c6*exp(c7*epsilon)*log(T*c8+1)*Abs(epsilon)**c9`. The last term is `exp(c7*epsilon)*log(T*c8+1)*epsilon**c9`. This mixes exp and power with log(T), can't separate to get both epsilon**3 and T*log(epsilon+1). **NO MATCH**

- **Candidate 42:** `T*c0*log(c1*Abs(epsilon)+1) + c2*exp(c3*epsilon) + c4*log(c5*exp(c6*epsilon)+1) + c7*epsilon**c8*log(c9*Abs(epsilon)+1)`. Has `T*log(epsilon+1)` ✓. Set c8=3: `c7*epsilon**3*log(c9*epsilon+1)` — this is epsilon**3*log(...), not pure epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

- **Candidate 47:** `c0*epsilon**2 + c1*exp(c2*epsilon) + c3*log(c4*Abs(epsilon)+1) + c5*(c6*Abs(epsilon)+1)**c7 + c8*epsilon*log(T*c9+1)`. The T-dependence is `c8*epsilon*log(T*c9+1)` which is NOT `T*log(epsilon+1)`. **NO MATCH**

After careful analysis of all 50 candidates, none have the right combination of `epsilon**3` (pure cubic) AND `T*log(epsilon+1)` without extra irreducible terms.
